    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary"><a class="link" href="https://az.linkedin.com/company/araz-supermarket-mmc?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Araz Supermarket MMC</a> və <a class="link" href="https://az.linkedin.com/company/oba-marketler-shebekesi?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>OBA Marketlər Şəbəkəsi</a>-nin birlikdə həyata keçirdiyi “Agile Team” layihəsi, <a class="link" href="https://az.linkedin.com/in/veyseloglu-group-of-companies-1912021a9?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Veyseloglu Group of Companies</a>-da ilin layihəsi elan olundu! 

Bu uğur, komandamızın çevik yanaşma, qarşılıqlı əməkdaşlıq və fədakar əməyinin nəticəsidir.
Şamaxıda keçirdiyimiz teambuilding ilə bu nailiyyəti qeyd etdik.

Növbəti mərhələdə isə, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/next4biz?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>next4biz </a>partnyorumuz ilə işlərə start veririk. Daha çevik və daha effektiv əməliyyatlar üçün birlikdə irəliləyirik!  
----
The “Agile Team” project, jointly implemented by the <a class="link" href="https://az.linkedin.com/company/araz-supermarket-mmc?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Araz Supermarket MMC</a>  and <a class="link" href="https://az.linkedin.com/company/oba-marketler-shebekesi?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>OBA Marketlər Şəbəkəsi</a>  teams to establish business processes, has been recognized as the Project of the Year within <a class="link" href="https://az.linkedin.com/in/veyseloglu-group-of-companies-1912021a9?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Veyseloglu Group of Companies</a>! This achievement was made possible thanks to our team’s agile mindset, strong collaboration, and dedicated effort.

We celebrated this success with a team-building event held in Shamakhı, strengthening our unity and shared vision.

In the next phase, we are partnering with <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/next4biz?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>next4biz </a>to digitize and systematize our business processes. Together, we are moving forward towards more agile and efficient operations!</p>

            <a class="text-sm link-styled no-underline leading-open px-0.25 outline-offset-[-1px]" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/teomanberkayayaz?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare_feed-actor-name" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare_feed-actor-name" aria-label="Teoman Berkay Ayaz adlı üyenin profilini görüntüleyin" data-tracking-will-navigate>
              Teoman Berkay Ayaz
            </a>
<!----><!---->        </div>

            <p class="!text-xs text-color-text-low-emphasis leading-[1.33333] px-0.25 m-0 truncate">
<!---->                Veri Bilimci &amp; Ar-Ge
            </p>

              <span class="!text-xs text-color-text-low-emphasis leading-[1.33333] px-0.25 flex">
                  <time class="flex-none">
                    

    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    

    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    

      3ay
  
                      <span aria-hidden="true" class="text-color-text-low-emphasis before:middot"></span>
                      <span>
                        Düzenlendi
                      </span>
                  </time>
<!---->              </span>
                </div>

<!---->    </div>
  

        
            
  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="feed-reshare-content__commentary">It pleases me to announce to you that our latest research paper here at the <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/next4biz?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Next4biz</a> R&amp;D Center, "Graph Based Business Process Anomaly Detection with Edge Feature Reconstruction and Advanced Linear Networks" is now available on IEEE Xplore through the link below.

<a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/gErg3wKa?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/gErg3wKa</a>

This study is part of an extensive research series conducted here at the <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/next4biz?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Next4biz</a> R&amp;D Center under the project AnomalyNet, a state-of-the-art business process anomaly detection framework aiming to help business users with their process inefficiencies.

Our study, presented at the 7th International Congress on Human-Computer Interaction, Optimization and Robotic Applications (ICHORA), is a continuation of a previous study presented at the International Computer Engineering Conference (UBMK). It expands upon its predecessor with a more informative graph construction scheme and a more complex neural network architecture.

If you wish to learn more about the software solutions developed here, feel free to check out our paper.</p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Exciting news from the Next4biz R&amp;D Center!

Our paper, "Multi-Graph Anomaly Detection in Business Processes with Scalable Neural Architectures," is now published in <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/showcase/ieee-access/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>IEEE Access</a>! 

This study advances AI-driven anomaly detection for BPM, improving detection accuracy by up to 22% while reducing computational costs by 50%. 

Key innovations include:
🔹 Multi-graph approach for better workflow analysis
🔹 Transformer-based decoders for efficiency &amp; precision
🔹 Denoising training for adaptable anomaly detection

Access the full paper here: <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dnD7hFhq?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dnD7hFhq</a>

At Next4biz, we’re committed to pioneering AI solutions in process automation. </p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Bir müşteri ilişkileri yöneticisi olarak gününüz nasıl geçiyor? 📞💬📧

Çağrılar, e-postalar, WhatsApp mesajları, sosyal medya yorumları derken, takip edilmesi gereken yüzlerce müşteri talebi… Peki, gerçekten süreci yönetiyor musunuz, yoksa sürecin içinde kayboluyor musunuz?

Çoğu şirket için müşteri hizmetleri, şikayetin alındığı anda değil, çözüme ulaştığı noktada tamamlanır. Ama gerçekte ne kadar kontrol sahibisiniz?
🔍 Müşteri taleplerinin hangi kanaldan geldiğini anlık olarak takip edebiliyor musunuz?
🔍 Şikayetlerin hangi aşamada olduğunu ve ne zaman çözüme ulaşacağını görebiliyor musunuz?
🔍 Aynı sorunların tekrarını önlemek için kök neden analizi yapabiliyor musunuz?

💡Eğer bu sorulara net cevaplar veremiyorsanız, müşteri hizmetlerini daha etkin yönetmek için sürecinizi gözden geçirmenin zamanı gelmiş olabilir. Neyse ki <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/next4biz?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>next4biz </a>var!</p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Ever feel like requests from business units get lost in translation? 
You’re not alone.
📋 Business teams explain what they need.
💻 IT designs and develops.
❓ Yet somehow, the final product still misses the mark.

So, what’s going wrong?
The real issue is the lack of prototyping. Without a clear, testable interface that bridges the gap between business and IT, it’s almost impossible to ensure the final result matches the original vision.

Here’s the solution:
With Next4biz BPM, you can seamlessly design, test, and prototype workflows. This ensures:
✅ Business and IT stay perfectly aligned.
✅ Workflows run smoothly from start to finish.
✅ The final product fits your business needs exactly.

Don’t let miscommunication cost you time, effort, and resources.
